=== sources/olden-era.com/text/en/units.txt ===
Units

In Heroes of Might and Magic: Olden Era, there is a huge variety of units. They can be divided into two major categories: factional (belonging to a specific town/castle) and neutral (independent).

Faction Units

These units are recruited in their native towns. Every week, towns generate growth (reinforcements), after which the units can be picked up into the army. When you construct a unit building, you immediately receive one growth stack (without bonuses).

Recruitment requires gold. T7 units also require other resources. The main feature of faction units is upgrades: build the corresponding upgrade building in the town, and each unit will have two upgrade options. They differ in appearance, stats, and abilities. You can freely switch between upgrades simply by visiting the town with the required building.

This adds depth: one upgrade might focus on high damage, while the other offers super-high initiative (to act first and use abilities before the enemy’s turn). Or utility units like Arbitr — both upgrades have powerful abilities, and you’ll want to have both in battle.

Neutral Units

They do not belong to any faction, appear on the adventure map or guard objects. They cannot be upgraded — only one version exists. Ways to obtain:

Hiring buildings (specialized)

Defeating guards at objects — units as reward

 []— reroll native troops with a chance to get neutral units

Summoning spells (temporary stacks on the battlefield)

Unit Tiers

Tier is a rough measure of power. Faction units: 7 tiers (T1 — cheap/weak, T7 — top/expensive). Higher tier = better stats, powerful abilities, easier to clear without losses.

Neutral units: 8 tiers. T8 are elite with insane difficulty (they guard treasures). In the beta, T8 does not drop from the Chimerologist’s Hut. The most common T8 is [Lich Dragon]: theBone ArmageddonBone ArmageddonDeals [ 0 × amount of units ] Pure Damage to all other creatures.ability deals 333 damage to all units in battle!

Unit Stats

11 key stats determine a unit’s balance and value:

health— health. How much damage the unit can take.

damage— base damage per hit (without modifiers).

attack— hero’s attack. Formula: (1 + 5% × ATK) — damage multiplier.

defence— hero’s defense. Formula: (1 + 5% × DEF) — reduces incoming damage.

initiative— turn order in the round. High value = acts earlier. “Wait” shifts the queue.

speed— movement range in combat (tiles).

morale— base morale (usually 0). Range depends on unit type. +1 = +4% chance of extra turn; -1 = chance to skip turn.

luck— base luck (usually 0). Range by unit type. +1 = +6% chance of extra damage; -1 = reduced damage.

growth— weekly growth (faction units only).

experience— EXP gained per unit on victory.

value— internal value for map balance (≈ EXP × 10, adjusted for rare cases).

Unit Abilities

In addition to stats, units have unique passive abilities (always active, e.g. [Hydra]hits multiple tiles withSweeping StrikeSweeping StrikeDeals Damage to the target and two adjacent hexes to its sides., [Griffin]flies withFlyingFlyingMovement ignores obstacles and traps.) and active abilities. Active abilities consume focus points accumulated during combat. Build up enough — boom, powerful effect!

Attack Types

Melee AttackMelee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.— melee

Ranged AttackRanged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).— ranged, across the entire field

Long ReachLong ReachHas an attack that targets the hex directly behind an adjacent hex. It doesn’t provoke counterattacks and doesn’t move the attacker next to their target.— ranged, but only 1 tile forward

Unit Types

Unit type determines morale/luck range, necromancy interaction, immunities to magic/abilities:

Hive SpawnHive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Hive Spawn count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

LivingLivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Living creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

Magic CreatureMagic CreatureA beast or beast‑like creature. Jadame’s beasts often have fantastical powers; denizens of other planes, even more so.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Magic Creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

EmbodimentEmbodimentA spirit, soul, or other intangible power that has coalesced into material form.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Embodiments do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

UndeadUndeadA creature or person whose life has been prolonged by unnatural means.

Morale: Always neutral.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Undead do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

巨龙巨龙强大且古老的生物，通常具有智能，体内蕴含神奇魔法。

士气范围：0 至 5
幸运范围：0 至 3

阵亡巨龙生物会计入战斗结束后的死灵术复苏强度。

ConstructConstructInert matter that has been reanimated with magic or other means.

Morale: Always neutral.
Luck: Always neutral.

Fallen Constructs do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.

Native Terrain

On home terrain, units gain +1 Initiative:

Temple: Grass

Necropolis: Deathland

Dungeon: Dirt

Schism: Snow

Hive: Lava

Sylvan: Autumn

Morale and Luck: Limits and Super Boosts

Each unit type has its own morale/luck cap. Example: [Swordsman](LivingLivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Living creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.) — max 5 (25% chance per the base formula of 4% per point). [Angel](EmbodimentEmbodimentA spirit, soul, or other intangible power that has coalesced into material form.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Embodiments do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.) — only 3 (15%).

The range cannot be changed, but you can boost the base modifier (increases the chance for all units):

Heroes: [Aeos the Exalted:], [Rhea:]

Set Knight’s Honor ( [Plate Armor], [Lance], [Misericorde], [Armet], [Барабан войны]) — +5%

Skills [Expert Leadership]/ [Expert Luck]: sub-skillsResolve:ResolveFriendly creatures’ chance to take an additional turn increases by 1% for each point of Morale. This bonus is doubled if the hero knows “Battlecraft.”+Beastly Confidence:Beastly ConfidenceFriendly creatures have a 1% higher chance to land a Lucky Strike for each point of Luck. This bonus is doubled if the hero knows “Primal Magic.”(synergy doubles the effect)

Laws:1EncouragementThe chance of Morale triggering for friendly creatures increases by 1% for each point of their Morale.(+2%)

Maximum boost: lvl 20 [Aeos the Exalted:](+7%) + set (+5%) + Resolve (+2%) +1EncouragementThe chance of Morale triggering for friendly creatures increases by 1% for each point of their Morale.(+2%) = 20% per point. [Swordsman]: 5 × 20% = 100% extra turn chance. [Angel]: 3 × 20% = 60%.

Units

Bewitcher Shoth

Tier5•Schism

health:60

attack:16

defence:13

damage:20–20

initiative:5

speed:6

morale:0

luck:0

growth:3

value:849

experience:94

Cost

780

Abilities

Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Living
LivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Living creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Nimbleness
NimblenessCan perform Ranged attacks even while adjacent to an enemy.
Earn Your Magic, Dear
Earn Your Magic, DearEnemy hero’s spells cost +2 mana. This effect does not stack; only the strongest one is active.
Duelist
DuelistReceives no penalty in Melee range, dealing full Damage.
Flog Idle Mind
Flog Idle MindDeals 66 Pure Damage per Focus Charge to target enemy creature.

Binder

Tier2•Schism

health:15

attack:6

defence:7

damage:4–5

initiative:5

speed:5

morale:0

luck:0

growth:12

value:184

experience:22

Cost

210

Abilities

Long Reach
Long ReachHas an attack that targets the hex directly behind an adjacent hex. It doesn’t provoke counterattacks and doesn’t move the attacker next to their target.
Living
LivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Living creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Glance of the Abyss
Glance of the AbyssCurses target enemy creature. Cursed creatures take [ 15 + 3 × amount of units ] Pure Damage at the start of their turn. This effect is stackable.
Duration: 2 round(s).
Abyssal Tendril
Abyssal TendrilDeals 50% of a basic attack ([ 2–2 × amount of units ]) as Pure Damage to target enemy creature and removes 1 of their counterattack charges.

Black Dragon

Tier7•Dungeon

health:350

attack:29

defence:31

damage:60–65

initiative:14

speed:9

morale:0

luck:0

growth:1

value:8009

experience:801

Cost

50002

Abilities

巨龙
巨龙强大且古老的生物，通常具有智能，体内蕴含神奇魔法。

士气范围：0 至 5
幸运范围：0 至 3

阵亡巨龙生物会计入战斗结束后的死灵术复苏强度。
Melee Attack
Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Flying
FlyingMovement ignores obstacles and traps.
Dragonbreath Strike
Dragonbreath StrikeDeals Damage to the target and any creature on the hex directly behind it.
Magic Immunity V
Magic Immunity VImmune to tier‑5 and lower spells.
Fighting Style: Sulfurous Assault
Fighting Style: Sulfurous AssaultPerforms a Cone Strike, dealing –50% Damage to each target.
Inner Flame
Inner FlameUntil the end of the next round, deals [ 30 × amount of units ] Magic Damage when attacked in Melee.
Fires of Dominion
Fires of DominionFriendly creatures gain 1 Morale and Luck; enemy creatures lose the same.

Units

Bloated Arbitrator

Tier6•Schism

health:75

attack:28

defence:22

damage:20–24

initiative:8

speed:5

morale:0

luck:0

growth:2

value:2259

experience:237

Cost

1900

Abilities

Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Living
LivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Living creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Paradoxical Shots
Paradoxical ShotsRanged penalties are reversed for this creature.
Attacks deal +10% Damage per hex (up to a maximum of +50%) if the target is more than 3 hexes away.
If the target is adjacent, performs a Melee attack, dealing +50% Damage.
Power of the Abyss
Power of the AbyssIncreases the hero’s maximum mana by 20. This effect does not stack.
Slimy Touch
Slimy TouchAttacks deal +[ 4 × amount of units ] Pure Damage and lower the target’s Speed and Initiative by 1 until the end of round. This effect does not stack.
Command: Switch Places
Command: Switch PlacesMakes any two creatures switch places, as long as they are within 8 hexes of one another.
Frozen Pages
Frozen PagesPrevents the enemy hero from using the Spellbook until the end of the round. This effect does not stack.

Units

Blooming Aqualotl

Tier4•Sylvan

health:35

attack:11

defence:9

damage:14–16

initiative:7

speed:6

morale:0

luck:0

growth:4

value:518

experience:60

Cost

500

Abilities

Embodiment
EmbodimentA spirit, soul, or other intangible power that has coalesced into material form.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Embodiments do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Blink
BlinkTeleports directly to destination hex, ignoring obstacles and traps.
Embodiment of Water
Embodiment of WaterThis creature leaves no body upon death. Immune to “Ice Bolt” and “Circle of Winter.”
Awaken: Water II
Awaken: Water IIThis creature gains 2 Speed and Initiative, 15 HP, and the ability to perform Ranged attacks even there is an adjacent enemy. Allows the use of other abilities. Once per battle; lasts until the end of battle.
Rivulet Retreat
Rivulet RetreatBlinks to any free hex within a 4‑hex range.

luck:0

growth:7

value:300

experience:36

Cost

320

Abilities

Hive Spawn
Hive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Hive Spawn count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Melee Attack
Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Flying
FlyingMovement ignores obstacles and traps.
Hivemind: Nest Protector
Hivemind: Nest ProtectorAt the start of battle, for each other unique Hive creature in the army, this creature’s Defense increases by 1. Upon death, this creature generates 2 Focus Point(s).
Whispers of Doubt
Whispers of DoubtAttacks cause the target to always deal minimal Damage.
Duration: 1 round(s).

Hive Spawn
Hive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.

Long Reach
Long ReachHas an attack that targets the hex directly behind an adjacent hex. It doesn’t provoke counterattacks and doesn’t move the attacker next to their target.
Hivemind: Vanguard
Hivemind: VanguardAt the start of battle, for each other unique Hive creature in the army, this creature’s Attack increases by 1. Whenever this creature kills an enemy, it generates 2 Focus Point(s).
Topple the Strong!
Topple the Strong!The higher the target’s tier, the more Damage this creature deals to it: +3% Damage per tier of difference.

Units

Hive Queen

Tier7•Hive

health:200

attack:25

defence:25

damage:60–60

initiative:7

speed:6

morale:0

luck:0

growth:1

value:3356

experience:336

Cost

22001

Abilities

Hive Spawn
Hive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Hive Spawn count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Melee Attack
Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Soul Assimilator
Soul AssimilatorAt the beginning of a battle, gains bonuses for each faction represented in the enemy’s army:

• Temple: +25% Attack
• Necropolis: +25% Defense
• Grove: +3 Luck and Morale
• Dungeon: +10% Damage
• Schism: +20% HP
• Neutral: +2 Speed
Beelzebub’s Agenda
Beelzebub’s AgendaThe hero deals +25% Magic Damage. This effect does not stack.
Squash the Weak!
Squash the Weak!The lower the target’s tier, the more Damage this creature deals to it: +3% Damage per tier of difference.
Blasphemous Adoration
Blasphemous AdorationDoubles this creature’s “Soul Assimilator” effects until the end of the next round.
Contaminating Blast
Contaminating BlastDeals 50% of a basic attack ([ 30–30 × amount of units ]) as Magic Damage to the target and all creatures within two hexes of it.

Abilities

Undead
UndeadA creature or person whose life has been prolonged by unnatural means.

Morale: Always neutral.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Undead do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Melee Attack
Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Death Stare
Death StareEach attack also kills +1 enemy unit(s) in addition to regular Damage. Works on creatures up to tier 7.
Dreadful Presence
Dreadful PresenceReduces all enemies’ Morale by 2. This effect does not stack; only the strongest one is active.
Hungering Hollow
Hungering HollowWhenever a friendly creature dies, this creature gains +3 Attack until the end of battle.
Reap Without Sowing
Reap Without SowingHits the target and all enemies adjacent to it.

=== sources/olden-era.com/text/en/units/polar_aqualotl.txt ===
Units

Polar Aqualotl

Tier4•Sylvan

health:35

attack:13

defence:9

damage:14–16

initiative:6

speed:5

morale:0

luck:0

growth:4

value:518

experience:60

Cost

500

Abilities

Embodiment
EmbodimentA spirit, soul, or other intangible power that has coalesced into material form.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Embodiments do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Blink
BlinkTeleports directly to destination hex, ignoring obstacles and traps.
Embodiment of Water
Embodiment of WaterThis creature leaves no body upon death. Immune to “Ice Bolt” and “Circle of Winter.”
Awaken: Water II
Awaken: Water IIThis creature gains 2 Speed and Initiative, 15 HP, and the ability to perform Ranged attacks even there is an adjacent enemy. Allows the use of other abilities. Once per battle; lasts until the end of battle.
Icy Veins
Icy VeinsAttacks prevent the target from restoring HP by any means until the end of the round.
Whirlpool
WhirlpoolConfuses the target enemy. While Confused, their Speed and Initiative are reduced by 2.
Duration: 3 round(s).

Pyroboros

Tier6•Hive

health:120

attack:20

defence:20

damage:21–23

initiative:9

speed:8

morale:0

luck:2

growth:2

value:2250

experience:236

Cost

1900

Abilities

Hive Spawn
Hive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Hive Spawn count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Blink
BlinkTeleports directly to destination hex, ignoring obstacles and traps.
Corpse Eater
Corpse EaterIf destination hex contains a fallen corpse, it is devoured, restoring 65 HP. This can revive fallen units.
Demonic Stench
Demonic StenchReduces enemy creatures’ Luck by 2. This effect does not stack; only the strongest one is active.
Duelist
DuelistReceives no penalty in Melee range, dealing full Damage.
Hivemind: Vanguard
Hivemind: VanguardAt the start of battle, for each other unique Hive creature in the army, this creature’s Attack increases by 1. Whenever this creature kills an enemy, it generates 2 Focus Point(s).

Abilities

Flying

Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Magic Creature
Magic CreatureA beast or beast‑like creature. Jadame’s beasts often have fantastical powers; denizens of other planes, even more so.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –5 to 5.

Fallen Magic Creatures count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Summoning Rite: Ra’Shoth
Summoning Rite: Ra’ShothOnce per battle, summons a stack of Ra’Shoth in place of a friendly corpse.
The summon has 50% HP of the corpse’s original stack and no more than [ current amount of summoners ] units. These creatures are permanent and remain after the battle.

100

Abilities

Hive SpawnA part of a hivemind that serves a powerful lord from beyond.

Morale range: –5 to 5.

Long Reach
Long ReachHas an attack that targets the hex directly behind an adjacent hex. It doesn’t provoke counterattacks and doesn’t move the attacker next to their target.
Hivemind: Vanguard
Hivemind: VanguardAt the start of battle, for each other unique Hive creature in the army, this creature’s Attack increases by 1. Whenever this creature kills an enemy, it generates 2 Focus Point(s).
Topple the Strong!
Topple the Strong!The higher the target’s tier, the more Damage this creature deals to it: +3% Damage per tier of difference.

Living

Paradoxical ShotsRanged penalties are reversed for this creature.

Abilities

Embodiment
EmbodimentA spirit, soul, or other intangible power that has coalesced into material form.

Morale range: –3 to 3.
Luck range: –3 to 3.

Fallen Embodiments do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Melee Attack
Melee AttackCan only attack adjacent enemies. Provokes counterattacks.
Area Strike
Area StrikeDeals Damage to the target and all hexes around it. Additional targets take –50% Damage.
Embodiment of Earth
Embodiment of EarthThis creature leaves no body upon death. Immune to “Cave In” and “Stone Fangs” spells.
Awaken: Earth I
Awaken: Earth IThis creature gains 2 Speed and Initiative, 10 HP, and unlimited counterattacks. Once per battle; lasts until the end of battle.

Abilities

Long Reach
Long ReachHas an attack that targets the hex directly behind an adjacent hex. It doesn’t provoke counterattacks and doesn’t move the attacker next to their target.
Living
LivingA fully sentient inhabitant of Jadame.

Morale range: –5 to 5.

Gaze of the Abyss: SluggishnessDeals 50% of a basic attack ([ 2–4 × amount of units ]) as Pure Damage to the target and all the adjacent enemies. All targets’ Initiative reduces by 1 until the end of next round.
Gaze of the Abyss: Slow
Gaze of the Abyss: SlowDeals 50% of a basic attack ([ 2–4 × amount of units ]) as Pure Damage to the target and all the adjacent enemies. All targets’ Speed reduces by 1 until the end of next round.

Abilities

Construct
ConstructInert matter that has been reanimated with magic or other means.

Morale: Always neutral.
Luck: Always neutral.

Fallen Constructs do NOT count towards the power of Necromancy reanimation after battle.
Ranged Attack
Ranged AttackCan attack enemies at any range. Replaced with a weaker Melee attack if an enemy is adjacent. –50% Melee Damage.
Targets 3 or more hexes away take –10% Damage per hex (up to –50%).
Duelist
DuelistReceives no penalty in Melee range, dealing full Damage.
Sharpshooter
SharpshooterRanged attacks deal full Ranged Damage at any range.
Magic Defense IV
Magic Defense IVTakes –90% Magic Damage.
Time Loop
Time LoopPlaces an invisible trap. When an enemy ground creature steps on it, the creature is transported back to its starting point and forced to end turn.
Duration: 2 rounds.
